0x0002bc1f	Communication Faults
0x0002bc3e	his DID tracks the communication faults detected by the communication driver software. Once the bits are set, they will remain set until a service 0x14 is run. Below is the mapping of the data. Each flag indicates which DTC it is associated with. The failure type of the DTC is in the byte title. Bytes with identical mappings are grouped. For signals mapping, signals are grouped according to message ID, any of signal is set in each group, corresponding bit will be set. Byte and Bit position: Format: Message ID - Message Name/Signal Name(DTC number) BYTE 1 (missing messages Bit0-7 -00) Bit7: 0x178 - EngineClimateData_MS1 (DTC 0xC10000) Bit6: 0x3B3 - BodyInfo_3_MS1 (DTC 0xC14000) Bit5: 0x40A- GGCC_Config_Mgmt_ID_1_MS1 (DTC 0xC14000) Bit4: 0x42A - BattPwr_Data_MS1 (DTC 0xC14000) Bit3: 0x42C - Batt_Mgmt_Data_MS1 (DTC 0xC14000) Bit2: 0x42E - EngineData_2_MS1 (DTC 0xC15100) Bit1: 0x3E0 - Personality_Data_MS1 (DTC 0xC15500) Bit0: unused BYTE 2 (missing messages Bit0-2 -00) Bit2: 0x3C4 - BodyInfo_MS1 (DTC 0xC14000) Bit1: 0x3E2 - Personality_APIM_Data_MS1 (DTC 0xC25300) Bit0: 0x358 - Clmt_Button_Stat4_MS1 (DTC 0xC25300) BYTE 2 ('Invalid' data state Bit3-5 -68) Bit5: 0x42A - BattUlo_U_Actl | PwrSrcUlo_I_Actl | PwSrcUlo_I_Mx (DTC 0xC42268) Bit4: 0x3B3 - Dimming_Lvl | LitVal | Parklamp_Status | Ignition_Status (DTC 0xC42268) Bit3: unused BYTE 2 ('Unknown' data state Bit6-7 -81) Bit7: unused Bit6: 0x3B3 - Dimming_Lvl | LitVal | Parklamp_Status | Ignition_Status | LifeCycMde_D_Actl | Backlit_LED_Status | CrashEvnt_D_Stat | Remote_Start_Status (DTC 0xC42281) BYTE 3 (QF - 'Not_Within_Specification' data state Bit0-2 -00) Bit2: 0x42E - Veh_V_ActlEng (DTC 0xC40100) Bit1: 0x178 - AirAmb_Te_Actl (DTC 0xC40100) Bit0: 0x3C4 - EngClnt_Te_Actl (DTC 0xC40100) BYTE 3 (QF - 'Faulty' Bit3-5 -68) Bit5: unused Bit4: unused Bit3: unused BYTE 3 (QF - 'No_Data_Exists' data state Bit6-7 -81) Bit7: unused Bit6: unused BYTE 4 (QF - 'No_Data_Exists' data state Bit0 -81) Bit0: unused BYTE 4 (UB - 'Unchanged_data' data state Bit1-7 -82) Bit7: unused Bit6: 0x42E - RstrnlmpactEvntStatus Bit5: 0x3C4 - EngClnt_Te_Actl | MetricActv_B_Actl | MetricActvTe_B_Actl (DTC 0xC40182) Bit4: 0x42E - Veh_V_ActlEng | EngAout_N_Actl | StopStrtStdby_D_Indic (DTC 0xC40182) Bit3: 0x3BC - PwSrcULo_Pc_Mx | PwSrcULoFalt_D_Stat | ApedPos_Pc_ActlArb (DTC 0xC40182) Bit2: 0x42A - BattUlo_U_Actl | PwSrcUlo_I_actl |

0x000ae339	Communication Faults
0x000ae358	his DID tracks the communication faults detected by the communication driver software. Once the bits are set, they will remain set until a service 0x14 is run. Below is the mapping of the data. Each flag indicates which DTC it is associated with. The failure type of the DTC is in the byte title. Bytes with identical mappings are grouped. For signals mapping, signals are grouped according to message ID, any of signal is set in each group, corresponding bit will be set. Byte and Bit position: Format: Message ID - Message Name/Signal Name(DTC number) BYTE 1 (missing messages Bit0-7 -00) Bit7: 0x178 - EngineClimateData_MS1 (DTC 0xC10000) Bit6: 0x3B3 - BodyInfo_3_MS1 (DTC 0xC14000) Bit5: 0x40A- GGCC_Config_Mgmt_ID_1_MS1 (DTC 0xC14000) Bit4: 0x42A - BattPwr_Data_MS1 (DTC 0xC14000) Bit3: 0x42C - Batt_Mgmt_Data_MS1 (DTC 0xC14000) Bit2: 0x42E - EngineData_2_MS1 (DTC 0xC15100) Bit1: 0x3E0 - Personality_Data_MS1 (DTC 0xC15500) Bit0: unused BYTE 2 (missing messages Bit0-2 -00) Bit2: 0x3C4 - BodyInfo_MS1 (DTC 0xC14000) Bit1: 0x3E2 - Personality_APIM_Data_MS1 (DTC 0xC25300) Bit0: 0x358 - Clmt_Button_Stat4_MS1 (DTC 0xC25300) BYTE 2 ('Invalid' data state Bit3-5 -68) Bit5: 0x42A - BattUlo_U_Actl | PwrSrcUlo_I_Actl | PwSrcUlo_I_Mx (DTC 0xC42268) Bit4: 0x3B3 - Dimming_Lvl | LitVal | Parklamp_Status | Ignition_Status (DTC 0xC42268) Bit3: unused BYTE 2 ('Unknown' data state Bit6-7 -81) Bit7: unused Bit6: 0x3B3 - Dimming_Lvl | LitVal | Parklamp_Status | Ignition_Status | LifeCycMde_D_Actl | Backlit_LED_Status | CrashEvnt_D_Stat | Remote_Start_Status (DTC 0xC42281) BYTE 3 (QF - 'Not_Within_Specification' data state Bit0-2 -00) Bit2: 0x42E - Veh_V_ActlEng (DTC 0xC40100) Bit1: 0x178 - AirAmb_Te_Actl (DTC 0xC40100) Bit0: 0x3C4 - EngClnt_Te_Actl (DTC 0xC40100) BYTE 3 (QF - 'Faulty' Bit3-5 -68) Bit5: unused Bit4: unused Bit3: unused BYTE 3 (QF - 'No_Data_Exists' data state Bit6-7 -81) Bit7: unused Bit6: unused BYTE 4 (QF - 'No_Data_Exists' data state Bit0 -81) Bit0: unused BYTE 4 (UB - 'Unchanged_data' data state Bit1-7 -82) Bit7: unused Bit6: 0x42E - RstrnlmpactEvntStatus Bit5: 0x3C4 - EngClnt_Te_Actl | MetricActv_B_Actl | MetricActvTe_B_Actl (DTC 0xC40182) Bit4: 0x42E - Veh_V_ActlEng | EngAout_N_Actl | StopStrtStdby_D_Indic (DTC 0xC40182) Bit3: 0x3BC - PwSrcULo_Pc_Mx | PwSrcULoFalt_D_Stat | ApedPos_Pc_ActlArb (DTC 0xC40182) Bit2: 0x42A - BattUlo_U_Actl | PwSrcUlo_I_actl |

   l  �did_FD10 � ��  2 � ����� �     �\ " �@����� �  � 2  �` ������This diagnostic session enables the default diagnostic session in the server(s) and does not support any diagnostic application timeout handling provisions (e.g., TesterPresent service is not necessary to keep the session active). A server shall always start the default diagnostic session when powered up. If no other diagnostic session is started, then the default diagnostic session shall be running as long as the server is powered.�
session_01�defaultSession�  �` ������ This diagnosticSession is used to enable timed diagnostic service functionality (e.g., I/O control). The diagnostic functionality in this session shall also include all supported diagnostic functionality supported in the defaultSession.�
session_03�extendedDiagnosticSession� ����service_22_p4_max_00�  �   �` �����EThis diagnosticSession enables all diagnostic services required to support the memory programming of a server. Regardless of whether the programmingSession runs in boot software or not, the ECU shall automatically suspend logging of DTCs and suspend transmission of non-diagnostic frames when entering the programmingSession.�
